Tuy nhi\u00ean, \u0111\u1ec3 th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng v\u1edbi qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o tr\u00ean X, b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n c\u00f3 m\u1ed9t chi\u1ebfn l\u01b0\u1ee3c qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3 v\u00e0 \u0111\u1eb7t m\u1ee5c ti\u00eau r\u00f5 r\u00e0ng.\n\nNgo\u00e0i ra, \u0111\u1ec3 t\u0103ng kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn v\u00e0 t\u01b0\u01a1ng t\u00e1c v\u1edbi kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng ti\u1ec1m n\u0103ng, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c c\u00e1ch sau \u0111\u00e2y:\n\n\ud83d\udd25S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng n\u1ec1n t\u1ea3ng qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o Google Ads \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea9y m\u1ea1nh th\u01b0\u01a1ng hi\u1ec7u c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n. V\u1edbi kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng hi\u1ec3n th\u1ecb tr\u00ean nhi\u1ec1u k\u00eanh kh\u00e1c nhau v\u00e0 \u0111\u1ebfn v\u1edbi \u0111\u1ed1i t\u01b0\u1ee3ng kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng m\u1ee5c ti\u00eau, Google Ads l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t trong nh\u1eefng c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3 nh\u1ea5t hi\u1ec7n nay.\n\n\ud83d\udd25X\u00e2y d\u1ef1ng m\u1ed9t trang web chuy\u00ean nghi\u1ec7p v\u00e0 t\u1ed1i \u01b0u h\u00f3a SEO \u0111\u1ec3 t\u0103ng kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng xu\u1ea5t hi\u1ec7n c\u1ee7a website c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n tr\u00ean c\u00e1c c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 t\u00ecm ki\u1ebfm. \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y gi\u00fap kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng d\u1ec5 d\u00e0ng t\u00ecm th\u1ea5y s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m ho\u1eb7c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n v\u00e0 t\u0103ng kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn v\u1edbi kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng ti\u1ec1m n\u0103ng.\n\n\ud83d\udd25S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng email marketing \u0111\u1ec3 gi\u1edbi thi\u1ec7u s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m ho\u1eb7c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n \u0111\u1ebfn kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng ti\u1ec1m n\u0103ng. Tuy nhi\u00ean, \u0111\u1ec3 th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng v\u1edbi email marketing, b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n c\u00f3 m\u1ed9t danh s\u00e1ch email ch\u1ea5t l\u01b0\u1ee3ng v\u00e0 n\u1ed9i dung email ph\u1ea3i h\u1ea5p d\u1eabn v\u00e0 c\u00f3 gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb cho ng\u01b0\u1eddi \u0111\u1ecdc.\n\n\ud83d\udd25T\u1ea1o n\u1ed9i dung ch\u1ea5t l\u01b0\u1ee3ng tr\u00ean c\u00e1c m\u1ea1ng x\u00e3 h\u1ed9i nh\u01b0 Facebook, Instagram, LinkedIn \u0111\u1ec3 t\u0103ng t\u01b0\u01a1ng t\u00e1c v\u00e0 ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn v\u1edbi kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng ti\u1ec1m n\u0103ng. B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd m\u1ea1ng x\u00e3 h\u1ed9i \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u0103ng b\u00e0i v\u00e0 qu\u1ea3n l\u00fd n\u1ed9i dung m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3.\n\n\ud83d\udd25Cu\u1ed1i c\u00f9ng, h\u00e3y th\u01b0\u1eddng xuy\u00ean \u0111\u00e1nh gi\u00e1 v\u00e0 \u0111o l\u01b0\u1eddng hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3 c\u1ee7a chi\u1ebfn d\u1ecbch qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o v\u00e0 \u0111i\u1ec1u ch\u1ec9nh khi c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea1t \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c k\u1ebft qu\u1ea3 t\u1ed1t nh\u1ea5t.\n\n\u2728C\u00e1ch th\u1ee9 hai l\u00e0 b\u00e1n s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m ho\u1eb7c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n tr\u00ean X. \u0110\u1ec3 b\u00e1n s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m ho\u1eb7c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 tr\u00ean X, b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n c\u00f3 m\u1ed9t t\u00e0i kho\u1ea3n X v\u1edbi l\u01b0\u1ee3ng ng\u01b0\u1eddi theo d\u00f5i \u0111\u00e1ng k\u1ec3. B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 nh\u01b0 X Ads ho\u1eb7c social media influencers \u0111\u1ec3 t\u0103ng l\u01b0\u1ee3ng ng\u01b0\u1eddi theo d\u00f5i c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh.\n\nNgo\u00e0i c\u00e1ch ti\u1ebfp th\u1ecb s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m ho\u1eb7c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 tr\u00ean X th\u00f4ng qua qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o tr\u1ea3 ph\u00ed ho\u1eb7c s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng social media influencers, b\u1ea1n c\u0169ng c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u00e1p d\u1ee5ng c\u00e1c chi\u1ebfn l\u01b0\u1ee3c kh\u00e1c \u0111\u1ec3 t\u0103ng hi\u1ec7u qu\u1ea3 b\u00e1n h\u00e0ng tr\u00ean n\u1ec1n t\u1ea3ng n\u00e0y, bao g\u1ed3m:\n\n\ud83d\udd25Chia s\u1ebb c\u00e1c \u0111\u00e1nh gi\u00e1 v\u00e0 ph\u1ea3n h\u1ed3i t\u00edch c\u1ef1c t\u1eeb kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng hi\u1ec7n t\u1ea1i c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n tr\u00ean X. Nh\u1eefng \u0111\u00e1nh gi\u00e1 t\u00edch c\u1ef1c n\u00e0y s\u1ebd gi\u00fap t\u0103ng s\u1ef1 tin t\u01b0\u1edfng v\u00e0 \u0111\u1ed9ng vi\u00ean ng\u01b0\u1eddi kh\u00e1c mua s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m ho\u1eb7c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n.\n\n\ud83d\udd25T\u1ea1o ra c\u00e1c n\u1ed9i dung h\u1ea5p d\u1eabn v\u00e0 \u0111\u1ed9c \u0111\u00e1o \u0111\u1ec3 thu h\u00fat s\u1ef1 ch\u00fa \u00fd c\u1ee7a kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng ti\u1ec1m n\u0103ng. H\u00e3y t\u00ecm hi\u1ec3u v\u00e0 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng nh\u1eefng hashtag ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn trong l\u0129nh v\u1ef1c c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n \u0111\u1ec3 t\u0103ng kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng ti\u1ebfp c\u1eadn v\u1edbi kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng ti\u1ec1m n\u0103ng.\n\n\ud83d\udd25Tham gia v\u00e0o c\u00e1c cu\u1ed9c tr\u00f2 chuy\u1ec7n v\u00e0 th\u1ea3o lu\u1eadn li\u00ean quan \u0111\u1ebfn l\u0129nh v\u1ef1c c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n tr\u00ean X. B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u01b0a ra c\u00e1c g\u00f3i qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o kh\u00e1c nhau, bao g\u1ed3m s\u1ed1 l\u01b0\u1ee3ng tweet, th\u1eddi l\u01b0\u1ee3ng qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o, \u0111\u1ed1i t\u01b0\u1ee3ng kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng nh\u1eafm t\u1edbi v\u00e0 gi\u00e1 c\u1ea3 ph\u00f9 h\u1ee3p.\n\n\ud83d\udd25B\u00e1n t\u00e0i kho\u1ea3n X : N\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 m\u1ed9t t\u00e0i kho\u1ea3n X v\u1edbi nhi\u1ec1u ng\u01b0\u1eddi theo d\u00f5i, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 b\u00e1n t\u00e0i kho\u1ea3n n\u00e0y \u0111\u1ec3 ki\u1ebfm ti\u1ec1n. C\u00e1c doanh nghi\u1ec7p ho\u1eb7c c\u00e1 nh\u00e2n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng t\u00e0i kho\u1ea3n c\u1ee7a b\u1ea1n \u0111\u1ec3 qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m ho\u1eb7c d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd v\u00e0 tr\u1ea3 ti\u1ec1n cho b\u1ea1n.\n\n\ud83d\udd25T\u1ea1o ra n\u1ed9i dung ch\u1ea5t l\u01b0\u1ee3ng cao: N\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t chuy\u00ean gia trong m\u1ed9t l\u0129nh v\u1ef1c n\u00e0o \u0111\u00f3, h\u00e3y t\u1ea1o ra c\u00e1c tweet ch\u1ea5t l\u01b0\u1ee3ng cao li\u00ean quan \u0111\u1ebfn l\u0129nh v\u1ef1c \u0111\u00f3 \u0111\u1ec3 thu h\u00fat ng\u01b0\u1eddi theo d\u00f5i. B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 b\u00e1n c\u00e1c tweet n\u00e0y cho c\u00e1c doanh nghi\u1ec7p ho\u1eb7c c\u00e1 nh\u00e2n c\u00f3 nhu c\u1ea7u qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o tr\u00ean X.\n\n\ud83d\udd25S\u1eed d\u1ee5ng X Ads: X cung c\u1ea5p m\u1ed9t d\u1ecbch v\u1ee5 qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o tr\u00ean n\u1ec1n t\u1ea3ng c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh. B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u1ea1o ra c\u00e1c qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o tr\u00ean X \u0111\u1ec3 thu h\u00fat kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng ti\u1ec1m n\u0103ng v\u00e0 t\u0103ng doanh s\u1ed1 b\u00e1n h\u00e0ng.\n\nD\u00f9 b\u1ea1n ch\u1ecdn ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ph\u00e1p n\u00e0o, h\u00e3y nh\u1edb lu\u00f4n th\u1ef1c hi\u1ec7n \u0111\u00fang c\u00e1c quy \u0111\u1ecbnh c\u1ee7a X v\u00e0 \u0111\u1ea3m b\u1ea3o r\u1eb1ng b\u1ea1n cung c\u1ea5p gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb th\u1ef1c cho kh\u00e1ch h\u00e0ng c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh.\n\n\u2728C\u00e1ch th\u1ee9 t\u01b0 l\u00e0 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng X \u0111\u1ec3 t\u1ea1o ra ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ti\u1ec7n truy\u1ec1n th\u00f4ng c\u1ee7a ri\u00eang b\u1ea1n. B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u1ea1o ra m\u1ed9t blog ho\u1eb7c trang web c\u1ee7a ri\u00eang m\u00ecnh v\u00e0 chia s\u1ebb n\u1ed9i dung c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh tr\u00ean X \u0111\u1ec3 thu h\u00fat l\u01b0\u1ee3ng ng\u01b0\u1eddi theo d\u00f5i \u0111\u00e1ng k\u1ec3. Sau \u0111\u00f3, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o tr\u00ean X \u0111\u1ec3 qu\u1ea3ng b\u00e1 cho ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ti\u1ec7n truy\u1ec1n th\u00f4ng c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh v\u00e0 ki\u1ebfm \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ti\u1ec1n t\u1eeb qu\u1ea3ng c\u00e1o.\n\nN\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n \u0111ang mu\u1ed1n t\u1ea1o n\u00ean m\u1ed9t ph\u01b0\u01a1ng ti\u1ec7n truy\u1ec1n th\u00f4ng c\u00e1 nh\u00e2n, X c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t c\u00f4ng c\u1ee5 h\u1eefu \u00edch \u0111\u1ec3 b\u1ea1n b\u1eaft \u0111\u1ea7u. So s\u00e1nh v\u1edbi c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n t\u01b0\u01a1ng t\u1ef1\n\n\u0110\u1ea7u ti\u00ean, b\u1ea1n n\u00ean so s\u00e1nh d\u1ef1 \u00e1n c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh v\u1edbi c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n t\u01b0\u01a1ng t\u1ef1 \u0111\u00e3 t\u0103ng gi\u00e1. Xem x\u00e9t lo\u1ea1i d\u1ef1 \u00e1n m\u00e0 b\u1ea1n \u0111ang xem x\u00e9t, v\u00ed d\u1ee5 nh\u01b0 c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n Layer1 th\u00ec h\u00e3y so s\u00e1nh v\u1edbi c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n Layer1 kh\u00e1c, Layer2 th\u00ec so s\u00e1nh v\u1edbi Layer2, v\u00e0 Memecoin th\u00ec so s\u00e1nh v\u1edbi Memecoin. H\u00e3y ph\u00e2n t\u00edch c\u00e1c y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 kh\u00e1c nhau gi\u1eefa hai d\u1ef1 \u00e1n \u0111\u1ec3 xem d\u1ef1 \u00e1n n\u00e0o m\u1ea1nh h\u01a1n v\u00e0 d\u1ef1 \u00e1n n\u00e0o y\u1ebfu h\u01a1n, t\u1eeb \u0111\u00f3 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 d\u1ef1 \u0111o\u00e1n gi\u00e1 c\u1ea3 v\u00e0 v\u1ed1n h\u00f3a c\u1ee7a ch\u00fang trong t\u01b0\u01a1ng lai. V\u00ed d\u1ee5, so s\u00e1nh gi\u1eefa Layer2 Op v\u00e0 Matic, b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n xem x\u00e9t nhi\u1ec1u y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 nh\u01b0 hi\u1ec7u su\u1ea5t trong m\u00f9a uptrend, c\u00f4ng ngh\u1ec7, h\u1ec7 th\u1ed1ng giao d\u1ecbch, v\u00e0 nhi\u1ec1u y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 kh\u00e1c n\u1eefa.\n\nTuy nhi\u00ean, c\u1ea7n l\u01b0u \u00fd r\u1eb1ng m\u1ed9t sai l\u1ea7m ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn l\u00e0 nhi\u1ec1u ng\u01b0\u1eddi ngh\u0129 r\u1eb1ng m\u1ed9t d\u1ef1 \u00e1n v\u1edbi Marketcap th\u1ea5p l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t c\u01a1 h\u1ed9i \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 t\u1ed1t. \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i l\u00fac n\u00e0o c\u0169ng \u0111\u00fang.\n\n2. Kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng \u0111\u1ea7u c\u01a1\n\nCrypto c\u00f3 b\u1ea3n ch\u1ea5t c\u1ee7a vi\u1ec7c \u0111\u1ea7u c\u01a1, v\u00e0 hi\u1ec7n nay, t\u00ednh \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng th\u1ef1c ti\u1ec5n c\u1ee7a n\u00f3 c\u00f2n r\u1ea5t h\u1ea1n ch\u1ebf. Do \u0111\u00f3, m\u1ed9t \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n c\u00f3 kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng \u0111\u1ea7u c\u01a1 t\u1ed1t th\u01b0\u1eddng c\u00f3 gi\u00e1 t\u0103ng m\u1ea1nh. M\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n c\u00f3 c\u01a1 ch\u1ebf \u0111\u1ea7u c\u01a1 t\u1ed1t nh\u01b0 BNB (\u0103n launchpad), Cake (c\u00f3 c\u01a1 ch\u1ebf farm \u0103n l\u00e3i k\u00e9p), AXS, v\u00e0 GMT c\u00f3 m\u00f4 h\u00ecnh ki\u1ebfm ti\u1ec1n th\u00fac \u0111\u1ea9y s\u1ef1 tham gia c\u1ee7a ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng v\u00e0 t\u0103ng gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu m\u1ea1nh m\u1ebd. Ngay c\u1ea3 c\u00e1c memecoin kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 \u1ee9ng d\u1ee5ng th\u1ef1c ti\u1ec5n v\u00e0 kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m n\u1ed5i tr\u1ed9i nh\u01b0 Doge v\u00e0 Shiba c\u0169ng c\u00f3 gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu t\u0103ng m\u1ea1nh nh\u1edd v\u00e0o c\u01a1 ch\u1ebf \u0111\u1ea7u c\u01a1.\n\n3. M\u00f4 h\u00ecnh ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng\n\nNh\u00ecn v\u00e0o c\u00e1c xu h\u01b0\u1edbng nh\u01b0 GameFi AXS v\u00e0 Move to Earn GMT, b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 th\u1ea5y r\u1eb1ng b\u1ea3n ch\u1ea5t c\u1ee7a ch\u00fang l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t lo\u1ea1i m\u00f4 h\u00ecnh Ponzi cao c\u1ea5p. M\u1ed9t d\u1ef1 \u00e1n n\u1ebfu c\u00f3 m\u00f4 h\u00ecnh ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng c\u00f3 xu h\u01b0\u1edbng Ponzi s\u1ebd c\u00f3 gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu t\u0103ng m\u1ea1nh. Vi\u1ec7c n\u00e0y \u0111\u00f2i h\u1ecfi ki\u1ebfn th\u1ee9c v\u1ec1 m\u00f4 h\u00ecnh n\u00e0y \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u01b0a ra quy\u1ebft \u0111\u1ecbnh \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0. B\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 v\u00e0o c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n Ponzi, nh\u01b0ng b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n c\u1ea3nh gi\u00e1c v\u00e0 r\u00fat ti\u1ec1n k\u1ecbp th\u1eddi khi th\u1ea5y t\u00edn hi\u1ec7u b\u00e1o \u0111\u1ecf.\n\n4. C\u01a1 h\u1ed9i l\u00e0m gi\u00e1, backer \u0111\u1ee9ng sau, v\u00e0 cap khi m\u1edbi ra s\u00e0n\n\nM\u1ed9t y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 quan tr\u1ecdng kh\u00e1c trong vi\u1ec7c \u0111\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 l\u00e0 th\u1eddi \u0111i\u1ec3m khi d\u1ef1 \u00e1n m\u1edbi \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c ni\u00eam y\u1ebft. V\u00ed d\u1ee5, SOL v\u00e0 AVAX, hai \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n Layer1, \u0111\u00e3 t\u0103ng t\u1eeb x100 \u0111\u1ebfn x200 t\u1eeb khi m\u1edbi ni\u00eam y\u1ebft. L\u00fd do ch\u00ednh l\u00e0 v\u00ec khi d\u1ef1 \u00e1n m\u1edbi ni\u00eam y\u1ebft, v\u1ed1n h\u00f3a th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng c\u1ee7a n\u00f3 th\u1ea5p, v\u00e0 n\u00f3 c\u00f3 s\u1ef1 h\u1ed7 tr\u1ee3 t\u1eeb c\u00e1c \u0111\u1ed1i t\u00e1c l\u1edbn nh\u01b0 Alameda Research. N\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u00ecm ra m\u1ed9t d\u1ef1 \u00e1n c\u00f3 kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng l\u00e0m gi\u00e1 t\u1ed1t, \u0111\u00f3 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t l\u1ef1a ch\u1ecdn \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 h\u1ea5p d\u1eabn. Tuy nhi\u00ean, b\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n ph\u1ea3i hi\u1ec3u r\u1eb1ng \u0111\u1ed9i l\u00e0m gi\u00e1 ph\u1ea3i c\u00f3 c\u01a1 s\u1edf \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ea9y l\u00ean gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu, v\u00e0 \u0111i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y li\u00ean quan \u0111\u1ebfn gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n.\n\n5. Gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n\n\n\u0110\u1ed1i v\u1edbi nh\u1eefng ng\u01b0\u1eddi y\u00eau th\u00edch \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 d\u00e0i h\u1ea1n, c\u00e1ch \u0111\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 t\u1ed1t nh\u1ea5t l\u00e0 d\u1ef1a tr\u00ean gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n. Gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb n\u00e0y d\u1ef1a tr\u00ean l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn m\u00e0 d\u1ef1 \u00e1n t\u1ea1o ra, kh\u00f4ng ph\u1ea3i l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn t\u1eeb vi\u1ec7c b\u00e1n token cho nh\u00e0 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0. V\u00ed d\u1ee5, Ethereum v\u00e0 Bitcoin c\u00f3 gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf t\u01b0\u01a1ng \u0111\u1ed1i cao v\u00ec ch\u00fang c\u00f3 kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng t\u1ea1o ra l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn t\u1eeb vi\u1ec7c c\u1ed9ng \u0111\u1ed3ng s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng n\u1ec1n t\u1ea3ng c\u1ee7a ch\u00fang \u0111\u1ec3 ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n kh\u00e1c. \u0110\u1ea7u t\u01b0 v\u00e0o c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n c\u00f3 kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng t\u1ea1o ra l\u1ee3i nhu\u1eadn d\u1ef1a tr\u00ean ho\u1ea1t \u0111\u1ed9ng c\u1ee7a n\u1ec1n t\u1ea3ng trong t\u01b0\u01a1ng lai c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch \u0111\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 h\u1ee3p l\u00fd.\n\n6. Tri\u1ec3n v\u1ecdng v\u00e0 ngu\u1ed3n thu c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n\n\nKhi \u0111\u00e1nh gi\u00e1 m\u1ed9t \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n, b\u1ea1n n\u00ean xem x\u00e9t c\u00f4ng ngh\u1ec7, ch\u1ee9c n\u0103ng, s\u1ef1 thu\u1eadn ti\u1ec7n v\u00e0 c\u00e1c \u01b0u \u0111i\u1ec3m c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n. H\u00e3y d\u1ef1 \u0111o\u00e1n s\u1ef1 th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n d\u1ef1a tr\u00ean kh\u1ea3 n\u0103ng ph\u00e1t tri\u1ec3n trong t\u01b0\u01a1ng lai. \u0110\u00e2y l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t l\u0129nh v\u1ef1c \u0111\u00f2i h\u1ecfi ki\u1ebfn th\u1ee9c v\u00e0 chuy\u00ean m\u00f4n cao. B\u1ea1n ph\u1ea3i hi\u1ec3u v\u00e0 nh\u1eadn th\u1ea5y \u0111i\u1ec1u \u0111\u1ed9c \u0111\u00e1o v\u00e0 gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb ri\u00eang bi\u1ec7t m\u00e0 d\u1ef1 \u00e1n mang l\u1ea1i. Tuy nhi\u00ean, b\u1ea1n c\u0169ng c\u1ea7n ph\u1ea3i xem x\u00e9t ngu\u1ed3n thu c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n, v\u00ec m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n c\u00f3 ngu\u1ed3n thu cao nh\u01b0ng gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu kh\u00f4ng t\u0103ng l\u00ean \u0111\u00e1ng k\u1ec3.\n\n7. M\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 kh\u00e1c\n\na. T\u00e0i s\u1ea3n c\u1ee7a nh\u00e0 s\u00e1ng l\u1eadp v\u00e0 qu\u1ef9 d\u1ef1 \u00e1n: \n\u0110\u00f4i khi, t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n c\u1ee7a nh\u00e0 s\u00e1ng l\u1eadp d\u1ef1 \u00e1n v\u00e0 qu\u1ef9 d\u1ef1 \u00e1n \u0111\u1ee9ng sau c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 gi\u00fap \u0111\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n.\n\nb. Th\u1eddi \u0111i\u1ec3m: \n\u0110\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n ph\u1ea3i ph\u1ee5 thu\u1ed9c v\u00e0o xu h\u01b0\u1edbng th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng. Trong th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng t\u00e0i ch\u00ednh, xu h\u01b0\u1edbng th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng c\u00f3 t\u00e1c \u0111\u1ed9ng l\u1edbn \u0111\u1ebfn gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu. B\u1ea1n c\u1ea7n x\u00e1c \u0111\u1ecbnh xem th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111ang trong giai \u0111o\u1ea1n t\u0103ng hay gi\u1ea3m \u0111\u1ec3 \u0111\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 m\u1ed9t c\u00e1ch ch\u00ednh x\u00e1c.\n\nc. C\u1ed9ng \u0111\u1ed3ng: \nC\u1ed9ng \u0111\u1ed3ng c\u1ee7a m\u1ed9t \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n c\u0169ng c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng \u0111\u1ebfn gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu. \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 kh\u00f4ng li\u00ean quan \u0111\u1ebfn gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb th\u1ef1c t\u1ebf c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n, nh\u01b0ng n\u1ebfu c\u00f3 m\u1ed9t c\u1ed9ng \u0111\u1ed3ng \u0111\u00f4ng \u0111\u1ea3o v\u00e0 t\u00edch c\u1ef1c, gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u0103ng l\u00ean do s\u1ef1 quan t\u00e2m t\u1eeb ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng.\n\nd. H\u01b0\u1edfng l\u1ee3i t\u1eeb s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n ho\u1eb7c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3: \nM\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 \u0111\u1ed3ng ti\u1ec1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u0103ng gi\u00e1 sau khi h\u01b0\u1edfng l\u1ee3i t\u1eeb s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n ho\u1eb7c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n c\u1ee5 th\u1ec3. V\u00ed d\u1ee5, vi\u1ec7c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n LDO h\u01b0\u1edfng l\u1ee3i t\u1eeb s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n c\u1eadp nh\u1eadt b\u1ea3n Shanghai c\u1ee7a Ethereum \u0111\u00e3 gi\u00fap n\u00f3 t\u0103ng gi\u00e1.\n\ne. Ni\u00eam y\u1ebft tr\u00ean s\u00e0n giao d\u1ecbch: \nS\u1ef1 ni\u00eam y\u1ebft tr\u00ean s\u00e0n giao d\u1ecbch c\u0169ng c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng \u0111\u1ebfn gi\u00e1 c\u1ed5 phi\u1ebfu. C\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n ni\u00eam y\u1ebft tr\u00ean c\u00e1c s\u00e0n l\u1edbn th\u01b0\u1eddng c\u00f3 gi\u00e1 cao h\u01a1n so v\u1edbi c\u00e1c d\u1ef1 \u00e1n ni\u00eam y\u1ebft tr\u00ean c\u00e1c s\u00e0n nh\u1ecf h\u01a1n.\n\nTr\u00ean \u0111\u00e2y l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 m\u00e0 b\u1ea1n c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 xem x\u00e9t khi \u0111\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 m\u1ed9t d\u1ef1 \u00e1n crypto. Tuy nhi\u00ean, c\u1ea7n l\u01b0u \u00fd r\u1eb1ng vi\u1ec7c \u0111\u1ecbnh gi\u00e1 crypto l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t qu\u00e1 tr\u00ecnh ph\u1ee9c t\u1ea1p v\u00e0 \u0111\u00f2i h\u1ecfi ki\u1ebfn th\u1ee9c s\u00e2u r\u1ed9ng v\u00e0 s\u1ef1 th\u1ea9m \u0111\u1ecbnh k\u1ef9 l\u01b0\u1ee1ng.\n#CryptoValuationExplained\n#BeyondTheCoinPrice\n#IntrinsicValueInvesting\n#Binance #Coinbase #Kraken #Bitfinex #Bittrex #Huobi #KuCoin #OKEx #Bitstamp #Gemini #FTX #BitFlyer #Poloniex #Gateio", "replyCount": 40, "retweetCount": 2, "likeCount": 58, "quoteCount": 0, "conversationId": 1709246609199132744, "hashtags": [], "cashtags": [], "mentionedUsers": [], "links": [], "viewCount": 2826, "retweetedTweet": null, "quotedTweet": {"id": 1709244673888518476, "id_str": "1709244673888518476", "url": "https://twitter.com/Mrvanthien/status/1709244673888518476", "date": "2023-10-03 16:31:01+00:00", "user": {"id": 4261974614, "id_str": "4261974614", "url": "https://twitter.com/Mrvanthien", "username": "Mrvanthien", "displayname": "Oliver", "rawDescription": "Navigating #Crypto #Bitcoin realms, imparting #Knowledge, scrutinizing #Markets. Uncovering new #Airdrops, #Retroactive insights. \nDM: https://t.co/luuSnkoiUD", "created": "2015-11-17 00:12:02+00:00", "followersCount": 2959, "friendsCount": 1845, "statusesCount": 4256, "favouritesCount": 16503, "listedCount": 5, "mediaCount": 133, "location": "Hanoi, Vietnam", "profileImageUrl": "https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_images/1223792831744991234/_cqaF4ib_normal.jpg", "profileBannerUrl": "https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_banners/4261974614/1696058298", "protected": null, "verified": false, "blue": true, "blueType": null, "descriptionLinks": [{"url": "http://t.me/Mrvanthien", "text": "t.me/Mrvanthien", "tcourl": "https://t.co/luuSnkoiUD"}], "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.User"}, "lang": "en", "rawContent": "HOW TO VALUE A CRYPTO PROJECT\n\nPeople often wonder why each coin in the crypto market has a different price. Is it set by exchanges or just due to the preferences of market participants? Why do some projects with good potential like GAL and BICO see decreasing stock prices, while GAL's revenue is impressive, it has backing from major investment funds, and its technology is not bad? Or, like LDO, which has few use-cases but a rising stock price. This article will explain the reasons behind these phenomena.\n\n**I. Why value a project?**\n\nIn the crypto world, we're always concerned about buying and selling prices. To buy low and sell high, we need to understand the true value of a project. While valuing a project based on current information to predict the future isn't always accurate, it can help us make informed guesses. If you don't understand the value of the coin you hold, even if bought at a low price, you might sell too early.\n\n1. **Compare with similar projects**\n\nFirst, compare your project with similar projects that have appreciated. If looking at Layer1 projects, compare it with other Layer1 projects; Layer2 with Layer2; and Memecoin with Memecoin. Analyze the differences to determine which project is stronger and which is weaker to predict their future prices and market capitalization. For instance, when comparing Layer2 Op and Matic, consider factors like performance in an uptrend, technology, trading systems, and other aspects.\n\nHowever, note that a common mistake is thinking a low Marketcap project is a good investment opportunity, which isn't always the case.\n\n2. **Speculation potential**\n\nCrypto inherently involves speculation, and its practical application is still limited. Thus, coins with good speculative potential often see significant price increases. Coins like BNB (benefiting from launchpad), Cake (with compound interest farming mechanism), AXS, and GMT have revenue models that drive user engagement and robust stock price growth. Even memecoins without practical application and standout products, like Doge and Shiba, see strong stock prices due to speculative mechanisms.\n\n3. **Business model**\n\nObserving trends like GameFi AXS and Move to Earn GMT, they resemble high-end Ponzi schemes. A project with a Ponzi-like business model will have a rapidly increasing stock price. This requires understanding these models to make investment decisions. You can invest in Ponzi projects, but be alert and withdraw funds timely upon red flags.\n\n4. **Market-making opportunities, backing, and initial cap**\n\nAnother key factor in valuation is the moment a project is listed. For example, SOL and AVAX, both Layer1 coins, surged from x100 to x200 since their initial listing. The primary reason is their low market cap at listing and backing from significant partners like Alameda Research. If you can identify a project with strong market-making potential, it could be an attractive investment. However, realize that market makers must have a basis to push up stock prices, related to the actual value of the project.\n\n5. **Project's intrinsic value**\n\nFor long-term investment enthusiasts, the best valuation method is based on the project's intrinsic value. This value depends on the profits the project generates, not profits from selling tokens to investors. For instance, Ethereum and Bitcoin have relatively high intrinsic values as they can profit from their platforms used to develop other projects. Investing in projects that can generate profits based on their future platform activities might be a reasonable valuation method.\n\n6. **Prospects and revenue sources**\n\nWhen evaluating a coin, consider its technology, functionality, convenience, and project advantages. Predict the project's success based on future growth potential. This requires deep expertise. Understand and recognize the unique value a project offers. However, also assess its revenue sources since some coins have high revenue but don't see significant stock price increases.\n\n7. **Other factors**\n\na. **Founder's assets and project funds**: \nSometimes, the assets of the project's founder and supporting funds can help determine coin value.\n\nb. **Timing**: \nCoin valuation depends on market trends. Market trends significantly impact stock prices. Identify if the market is in a bullish or bearish phase to value accurately.\n\nc. **Community**: \nA coin's community can influence its stock price. This might not relate to the project's actual value, but if there's a large, active community, stock prices might rise due to user interest.\n\nd. **Benefits from specific events or projects**: \nSome coins might appreciate after benefiting from specific events or projects. For example, LDO profiting from Ethereum's Shanghai update caused its price to rise.\n\ne. **Exchange listing**:\nListing on exchanges can influence stock prices. Projects listed on larger exchanges tend to have higher prices than those on smaller ones.\n#CryptoValuationExplained\n#BeyondTheCoinPrice\n#IntrinsicValueInvesting", "replyCount": 0, "retweetCount": 0, "likeCount": 0, "quoteCount": 1, "conversationId": 1709244673888518476, "hashtags": [], "cashtags": [], "mentionedUsers": [], "links": [], "viewCount": null, "retweetedTweet": null, "quotedTweet": null, "place": null, "coordinates": null, "inReplyToTweetId": null, "inReplyToUser": null, "source": "<a href=\"https://mobile.twitter.com\" rel=\"nofollow\">Twitter Web App</a>", "sourceUrl": "https://mobile.twitter.com", "sourceLabel": "Twitter Web App", "media": {"photos": [{"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F7h0og0bcAASRdz.jpg"}], "videos": [], "animated": []}, "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.Tweet"}, "place": null, "coordinates": null, "inReplyToTweetId": null, "inReplyToUser": null, "source": "<a href=\"https://mobile.twitter.com\" rel=\"nofollow\">Twitter Web App</a>", "sourceUrl": "https://mobile.twitter.com", "sourceLabel": "Twitter Web App", "media": {"photos": [{"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F7h1IFTakAAEapo.jpg"}], "videos": [], "animated": []}, "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.Tweet"}

{"id": 1709244673888518476, "id_str": "1709244673888518476", "url": "https://twitter.com/Mrvanthien/status/1709244673888518476", "date": "2023-10-03 16:31:01+00:00", "user": {"id": 4261974614, "id_str": "4261974614", "url": "https://twitter.com/Mrvanthien", "username": "Mrvanthien", "displayname": "Oliver", "rawDescription": "Navigating #Crypto #Bitcoin realms, imparting #Knowledge, scrutinizing #Markets. Uncovering new #Airdrops, #Retroactive insights. \nDM: https://t.co/luuSnkoiUD", "created": "2015-11-17 00:12:02+00:00", "followersCount": 2959, "friendsCount": 1845, "statusesCount": 4256, "favouritesCount": 16503, "listedCount": 5, "mediaCount": 133, "location": "Hanoi, Vietnam", "profileImageUrl": "https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_images/1223792831744991234/_cqaF4ib_normal.jpg", "profileBannerUrl": "https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_banners/4261974614/1696058298", "protected": null, "verified": false, "blue": true, "blueType": null, "descriptionLinks": [{"url": "http://t.me/Mrvanthien", "text": "t.me/Mrvanthien", "tcourl": "https://t.co/luuSnkoiUD"}], "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.User"}, "lang": "en", "rawContent": "HOW TO VALUE A CRYPTO PROJECT\n\nPeople often wonder why each coin in the crypto market has a different price. Is it set by exchanges or just due to the preferences of market participants? Why do some projects with good potential like GAL and BICO see decreasing stock prices, while GAL's revenue is impressive, it has backing from major investment funds, and its technology is not bad? Or, like LDO, which has few use-cases but a rising stock price. This article will explain the reasons behind these phenomena.\n\n**I. Why value a project?**\n\nIn the crypto world, we're always concerned about buying and selling prices. To buy low and sell high, we need to understand the true value of a project. While valuing a project based on current information to predict the future isn't always accurate, it can help us make informed guesses. If you don't understand the value of the coin you hold, even if bought at a low price, you might sell too early.\n\n1. **Compare with similar projects**\n\nFirst, compare your project with similar projects that have appreciated. If looking at Layer1 projects, compare it with other Layer1 projects; Layer2 with Layer2; and Memecoin with Memecoin. Analyze the differences to determine which project is stronger and which is weaker to predict their future prices and market capitalization. For instance, when comparing Layer2 Op and Matic, consider factors like performance in an uptrend, technology, trading systems, and other aspects.\n\nHowever, note that a common mistake is thinking a low Marketcap project is a good investment opportunity, which isn't always the case.\n\n2. **Speculation potential**\n\nCrypto inherently involves speculation, and its practical application is still limited. Thus, coins with good speculative potential often see significant price increases. Coins like BNB (benefiting from launchpad), Cake (with compound interest farming mechanism), AXS, and GMT have revenue models that drive user engagement and robust stock price growth. Even memecoins without practical application and standout products, like Doge and Shiba, see strong stock prices due to speculative mechanisms.\n\n3. **Business model**\n\nObserving trends like GameFi AXS and Move to Earn GMT, they resemble high-end Ponzi schemes. A project with a Ponzi-like business model will have a rapidly increasing stock price. This requires understanding these models to make investment decisions. You can invest in Ponzi projects, but be alert and withdraw funds timely upon red flags.\n\n4. **Market-making opportunities, backing, and initial cap**\n\nAnother key factor in valuation is the moment a project is listed. For example, SOL and AVAX, both Layer1 coins, surged from x100 to x200 since their initial listing. The primary reason is their low market cap at listing and backing from significant partners like Alameda Research. If you can identify a project with strong market-making potential, it could be an attractive investment. However, realize that market makers must have a basis to push up stock prices, related to the actual value of the project.\n\n5. **Project's intrinsic value**\n\nFor long-term investment enthusiasts, the best valuation method is based on the project's intrinsic value. This value depends on the profits the project generates, not profits from selling tokens to investors. For instance, Ethereum and Bitcoin have relatively high intrinsic values as they can profit from their platforms used to develop other projects. Investing in projects that can generate profits based on their future platform activities might be a reasonable valuation method.\n\n6. **Prospects and revenue sources**\n\nWhen evaluating a coin, consider its technology, functionality, convenience, and project advantages. Predict the project's success based on future growth potential. This requires deep expertise. Understand and recognize the unique value a project offers. However, also assess its revenue sources since some coins have high revenue but don't see significant stock price increases.\n\n7. **Other factors**\n\na. **Founder's assets and project funds**: \nSometimes, the assets of the project's founder and supporting funds can help determine coin value.\n\nb. **Timing**: \nCoin valuation depends on market trends. Market trends significantly impact stock prices. Identify if the market is in a bullish or bearish phase to value accurately.\n\nc. **Community**: \nA coin's community can influence its stock price. This might not relate to the project's actual value, but if there's a large, active community, stock prices might rise due to user interest.\n\nd. **Benefits from specific events or projects**: \nSome coins might appreciate after benefiting from specific events or projects. For example, LDO profiting from Ethereum's Shanghai update caused its price to rise.\n\ne. **Exchange listing**:\nListing on exchanges can influence stock prices.
